# <a name="com-error-codes-security-and-setup"></a><span data-ttu-id="3c4c4-104">COM 錯誤碼 (安全性和設定) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c4c4-104">COM Error Codes (Security and Setup)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c4c4-105">下表提供以 COM 為基礎的 Api 所使用的錯誤碼清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c4c4-105">The following table provides a list of error codes used by COM-based APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c4c4-106">如果您在安裝或執行的應用程式遇到困難，請洽詢客戶對顯示錯誤訊息之軟體的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c4c4-106">If you are experiencing difficulty with an application you are installing or running, contact customer support for the software that is displaying the error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c4c4-107">若要取得 Microsoft 產品的支援，請移至 [https://support.microsoft.com](https://support.microsoft.com) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c4c4-107">To obtain support for a Microsoft product, go to [https://support.microsoft.com](https://support.microsoft.com).</span></span>
